342:   function distKm(a, b){
343:     const R = 6371;
344:     const toRad = d => d * Math.PI / 180;
345:     const dLat = toRad(b.lat - a.lat);
346:     const dLng = toRad(b.lng - a.lng);
347:     const la1 = toRad(a.lat);
348:     const la2 = toRad(b.lat);
349:     const h = Math.sin(dLat/2)**2 + Math.cos(la1) * Math.cos(la2) * Math.sin(dLng/2)**2;
350:     return 2 * R * Math.asin(Math.sqrt(h));
351:   }

1814:   function distKm(a,b){
1815:     const R = 6371;
1816:     const toRad = x => x * Math.PI / 180;
1817:     const dLat = toRad(Number(b.lat) - Number(a.lat));
1818:     const dLng = toRad(Number(b.lng) - Number(a.lng));

1824:       Math.cos(lat1) * Math.cos(lat2) *
1825:       Math.sin(dLng/2) * Math.sin(dLng/2);

335:   function hasCoord(stop){
336:     if(!stop) return false;
337:     const lat = parseFloat(stop.lat);
338:     const lng = parseFloat(stop.lng);
339:     return Number.isFinite(lat) && Number.isFinite(lng);

341: 
342:   function distKm(a, b){
343:     const R = 6371;
344:     const toRad = d => d * Math.PI / 180;
345:     const dLat = toRad(b.lat - a.lat);
346:     const dLng = toRad(b.lng - a.lng);
347:     const la1 = toRad(a.lat);
348:     const la2 = toRad(b.lat);
349:     const h = Math.sin(dLat/2)**2 + Math.cos(la1) * Math.cos(la2) * Math.sin(dLng/2)**2;
350:     return 2 * R * Math.asin(Math.sqrt(h));
351:   }

341: 
342:   function distKm(a, b){
343:     const R = 6371;
344:     const toRad = d => d * Math.PI / 180;
345:     const dLat = toRad(b.lat - a.lat);
346:     const dLng = toRad(b.lng - a.lng);
347:     const la1 = toRad(a.lat);
348:     const la2 = toRad(b.lat);
349:     const h = Math.sin(dLat/2)**2 + Math.cos(la1) * Math.cos(la2) * Math.sin(dLng/2)**2;
350:     return 2 * R * Math.asin(Math.sqrt(h));
351:   }

1808:   function formatKm(km){
1809:     if(!Number.isFinite(km) || km < 0) return "—";
1810:     if(km < 1) return Math.round(km * 1000) + " m";
1811:     return km.toFixed(2) + " km";
1812:   }
1813: 
1814:   function distKm(a,b){
1815:     const R = 6371;
1816:     const toRad = x => x * Math.PI / 180;
1817:     const dLat = toRad(Number(b.lat) - Number(a.lat));
1818:     const dLng = toRad(Number(b.lng) - Number(a.lng));
1819:     const lat1 = toRad(Number(a.lat));
1820:     const lat2 = toRad(Number(b.lat));
1821: 
1822:     const h =
1823:       Math.sin(dLat/2) * Math.sin(dLat/2) +
1824:       Math.cos(lat1) * Math.cos(lat2) *
1825:       Math.sin(dLng/2) * Math.sin(dLng/2);
1826: 
1827:     return 2 * R * Math.atan2(Math.sqrt(h), Math.sqrt(1-h));
1828:   }

28:   function norm(v){
29:     return text(v)
30:       .trim()
31:       .toLocaleLowerCase("tr-TR")
32:       .replace(/[–—_\/\\.,()[\]]/g, " ")
33:       .replace(/\s+/g, " ");
34:   }
35: 
36:   function distKm(a, b){
37:     const R = 6371;
38:     const toRad = d => d * Math.PI / 180;
39:     const dLat = toRad(Number(b.lat) - Number(a.lat));
40:     const dLng = toRad(Number(b.lng) - Number(a.lng));
41:     const la1 = toRad(Number(a.lat));
42:     const la2 = toRad(Number(b.lat));
43:     const h =
44:       Math.sin(dLat / 2) ** 2 +
45:       Math.cos(la1) * Math.cos(la2) * Math.sin(dLng / 2) ** 2;
46: 
47:     return 2 * R * Math.asin(Math.sqrt(h));
48:   }

===== 4) ANDROID / WEB KOPYA DURUMU =====
AYNI: templates/continue_trip.html <-> android_app/app/src/main/python/templates/continue_trip.html
YOK/YOK: static/continue_trip_core.js <-> android_app/app/src/main/python/static/continue_trip_core.js
AYNI: static/app.js <-> android_app/app/src/main/python/static/app.js
AYNI: templates/seats.html <-> android_app/app/src/main/python/templates/seats.html
AYNI: static/seats/seats.js <-> android_app/app/src/main/python/static/seats/seats.js
